# Expansion Art Guide -- Ragnarok Card Game
## AI Art Generation Reference (ALL Remaining Cards: Neutral, Norse Set, Old Gods, Tokens, Dragons, Beasts, Combo/Control, Artifacts, Armor)

Each entry includes: **Card ID**, **Type/Rarity/Cost**, **Stats**, **Flavor Text**, **Visual Art Prompt**, and **Key Visual Attributes**.

**Art Style Note for Minions:** Show the creature/character as a half-body or full-body portrait, filling 70-80% of the frame. Background should reflect their realm or lore origin. Use cinematic fantasy illustration style with rich texture and dramatic lighting. The character should feel alive -- caught in a moment of action or quiet intensity.

**Art Style Note for Spells:** Show the magical effect itself -- energy, runes, elemental forces, or cosmic phenomena. No characters should dominate the frame (they may appear as silhouettes or small figures for scale). The spell should feel like a moment frozen in time.

**Art Style Note for Artifacts & Weapons:** Show the legendary weapon or item as a centered object, radiating power. Meticulous craftsmanship detail, surrounded by its elemental aura or divine energy.

**Art Style Note for Armor:** Show the armor piece alone or on a mannequin/stand, emphasizing craftsmanship, material textures, and enchantment glows.

**Art Style Note for Tokens:** Simpler compositions with bold silhouettes. Quick-read visual identity at small card sizes.

---

# PART 1: COMMON NEUTRAL MINIONS

---

### Sea Sprite Raider (ID: 1001)
- **Type**: Minion (Naga) | **Rarity**: Common | **Cost**: 1
- **Stats**: 2/1
- **Flavor Text**: "From the depths of Aegir's realm, they come with shells as shields!"
- **AI Art Prompt**: Sea Sprite Raider, a Naga creature, in a dramatic battle-ready stance, set against the depths of the World Ocean. Evoking: "From the depths of Aegir's realm, they come with shells as shields!" Color palette: ocean blue, seafoam green, pearl white, deep teal.
- **Key Visual Attributes**:
  - Aquatic features with coral/shell motifs
  - Color: ocean blue dominant
  - Cinematic dramatic lighting
  - Common-appropriate visual intensity
  - Norse mythological design motifs

- **Type**: Minion (Dragon) | **Rarity**: Rare | **Cost**: 5
- **Stats**: 4/4
- **Effect**: Spell Damage +1. Battlecry: Draw a card.
- **Flavor Text**: "Young kin of Níðhöggr, the dragon who gnaws at Yggdrasil's roots."
- **AI Art Prompt**: Distinct and memorable with subtle magical accents. Nidhogg Whelp, a Dragon creature, mouth open in thunderous war cry, power radiating outward, set against a mythological Norse landscape. Evoking: "Young kin of Níðhöggr, the dragon who gnaws at Yggdrasil's roots." Color palette: emerald green, bark brown, golden amber, leaf gold.
- **Key Visual Attributes**:
  - Draconic scales, wings, breath element
  - Visible shockwave from war cry
  - Arcane energy at fingertips
  - Floating scrolls or cards nearby
  - Color: emerald green dominant

  - Color: fur brown dominant
